		tag = SOV

			limit = { JAP = { is_subject = no } }
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
		}
		else = { always = yes }
		
		AND = {
			761 = { is_controlled_by = event_target:WTT_communist_china }
			1008 = { is_controlled_by = event_target:WTT_communist_china }
			608 = { is_controlled_by = event_target:WTT_communist_china }
		}
		AND = {
			330 = { is_controlled_by = event_target:WTT_communist_china }
			657 = { is_controlled_by = event_target:WTT_communist_china }
			408 = { is_controlled_by = event_target:WTT_communist_china }
			
			563 = { is_controlled_by = event_target:WTT_communist_china }
			561 = { is_controlled_by = event_target:WTT_communist_china }
			409 = { is_controlled_by = event_target:WTT_communist_china }
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	option = {
		name = rcmsoviet.1001.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		event_target:WTT_communist_china = {
			country_event = { days = 5 id = rcmchina.226 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = retreat_from_CHI
		}
	}
}

	}

			base = 1
		}

			limit = {
				is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_ally = yes
				owner = { is_literally_china = yes has_war_with = root }
			}
			add_core_of = root
			transfer_state_to = root
		}
		
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					is_literally_china = yes
					or = { tag = root has_war_together_with = root tag = FROM has_war_together_with = FROM }
					controller = {
						is_literally_china = yes
						has_War_with = PREV
						or = { tag = root has_war_together_with = root tag = FROM has_war_together_with = FROM }
					}
				}
			}
			controller = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		
		white_peace = FROM
		remove_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = hostile_status }
		FROM = {
			remove_opinion_modifier = { target = root modifier = hostile_status }
		}
		set_global_flag = CHI_unite_PRC
		set_global_flag = second_unite_bypass
		FROM = { unlock_national_focus = CHI_Truce_of_the_Civil_War }
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = FROM
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
        }
		set_truce = { target = FROM days = 365 }
		
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = CHI
					NOT = { tag = CHI }
				}
				white_peace = PRC
				white_peace = GXC
				white_peace = GUD
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = PRC
					NOT = { tag = PRC }
				}
				white_peace = CHI
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = CHI
					relation = non_aggression_pact
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		add_stability = -0.10
		add_war_support = -0.10

		FROM = {
			white_peace = JAP
			give_military_access = JAP

		}

		every_unit_leader = { set_nationality = ROOT }
		}
		ROOT = {
		annex_country = { target = FROM transfer_troops = yes }
		}
		FROM = {
		if = {
	    limit = {
	    is_ai = no
	    }
	    ROOT = { change_tag_from = FROM }
	    }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #xinjiang tong die
	id = fate_of_jiajizhanfan.62
	title = fate_of_jiajizhanfan.62.t
	desc = fate_of_jiajizhanfan.62.desc
	
	trigger = {
	    
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
	    
	}
	
	option = {
		name = fate_of_jiajizhanfan.62.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		every_army_leader = { set_nationality = FROM }
		every_unit_leader = { set_nationality = FROM }
		if = {
		limit = { has_character = PRC_maozemin }
		PRC_maozemin = { set_nationality = FROM }
		PRC_chentanqiu = { set_nationality = FROM }
		}
		FROM = {
		annex_country = { target = ROOT transfer_troops = yes }
		}
		if = {
	    limit = {
	    is_ai = no
	    }
	    FROM = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
	    }
	}
	option = {
		name = fate_of_jiajizhanfan.62.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		FROM = {
		create_wargoal = {
			target = ROOT
			type = take_core_state
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
		type = antagonize
		id = root
		value = 9999
	    }
		add_ai_strategy = {
		type = conquer
		id = root
		value = 9999
	    }
		}
	}
}

	option = {
		name = prc_yanan.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
		1030 = {
		teleport_armies = { 
				to_state = 744
			}
		}
		if = {
		limit = {
		not = { controls_state = 622 }
		}
		622 = {
		set_demilitarized_zone = no
		clr_state_flag = I_choose_this_state_to_DMZ
		remove_core_of = NEA
		teleport_armies = { 
				to_state = 744
			}
		}
		transfer_state = 622
		}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		1030 = {
		set_demilitarized_zone = no
		clr_state_flag = I_choose_this_state_to_DMZ
		remove_core_of = NEA
		}
		}
		
		1030 = {
			set_state_name = yanan
		}
		set_province_name = { id = 13405 name = "延安" }
		
		transfer_state = 1030
		set_capital = { state = 1030 }
		
		1030 = {
			set_victory_points = {
				province = 13405
				value = 10
			}
			#add_building_construction = {
			#	type = bunker
			#	level = 5
			#	province = 13405
			#	instant_build = yes
			#}
		
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex level = 2 instant_build = yes
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory level = 1 instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		
		add_political_power = 25
		
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = { id = prc_yanan.2 hours = 2 }
		country_event = { id = prc_yanan.2 days = 1 }
		}
		
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 500
						producer = NEA
					}
		custom_effect_tooltip = receive_6k_ammo
		add_to_variable = { ammunition_variable = 6 }			
	}
	
}

add_namespace = zizhi_hidden_event
news_event = {
	id = zizhi_hidden_event.1
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
	    any_country = { exists = yes has_war = no owns_state = 527 or = { is_ally_with = SOV is_ally_with = event_target:WTT_communist_china } or = { original_tag = KOR original_tag = DPR } }
		any_country = { exists = yes has_war = no owns_state = 1001 or = { is_ally_with = USA is_ally_with = event_target:nato_leader } or = { original_tag = KOR original_tag = DPR } }
		not = { any_country = { exists = yes or = { original_tag = KOR original_tag = DPR } has_government = n_socialism } }
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = no
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
	    random_country = {
		limit = { exists = yes has_war = no owns_state = 527 or = { is_ally_with = SOV is_ally_with = event_target:WTT_communist_china } or = { original_tag = KOR original_tag = DPR } }
		transfer_state = 1003 transfer_state = 527 transfer_state = 1004
		add_political_power = 1000
		}
		random_country = {
		limit = { exists = yes has_war = no owns_state = 1001 or = { is_ally_with = USA is_ally_with = event_target:nato_leader } or = { original_tag = KOR original_tag = DPR } }
		transfer_state = 525 transfer_state = 1002 transfer_state = 999 transfer_state = 1000 transfer_state = 1001
		add_political_power = 1000
		}
	}

	option = {
		
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = zizhi_hidden_event.3
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
	    has_global_flag = WW2modded
		not = { any_country = { is_major = yes is_faction_leader = yes is_subject = no has_war_with_major = yes } }
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = no
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
	    random_country = {
		limit = { is_major = yes is_faction_leader = yes is_subject = no num_of_factories > 500 is_democratic_type = yes }
		    add_named_threat = {
			threat = -50
			name = end_of_ww2
			}
		}
		random_country = {
		limit = { is_major = yes is_faction_leader = yes is_subject = no num_of_factories > 500 has_government = communism }
		    add_named_threat = {
			threat = -50
			name = end_of_ww2
			}
		}
		random_country = {
		limit = { is_major = yes is_faction_leader = yes is_subject = no num_of_factories > 500 has_government = fascism }
		    add_named_threat = {
			threat = -50
			name = end_of_ww2
			}
		}
		random_country = {
		limit = { is_major = yes is_faction_leader = yes is_subject = no num_of_factories > 500 has_government = neutrality }
		    add_named_threat = {
			threat = -50
			name = end_of_ww2
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = zizhi_hidden_event.5
	hidden = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 2 }
	title = ""
	desc = ""
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
			tag = SOV
			any_other_country = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				is_major = yes
				is_democratic_type = yes
				has_war_with = GER
				has_war_together_with = root #guo
				not = { has_war_with = root }
			}
			
			or = {
			has_government = communism
			is_democratic_type = yes
			}
			is_faction_leader = yes
			is_subject = no
			has_war_with = GER
			not = { has_global_flag = SOV_BAD_GUYS_flag } #guo
			not = { has_global_flag = address_cooperation_with_allies_zz } #guo
	}
	immediate = {
		activate_mission = SOV_join_allies_decision
		set_global_flag = SOV_join_allies_decision_will_happen
	}
}

	id = zizhi_hidden_event.6

		not = { country_exists = NEA }

		PRC = { NOT = { any_unit_leader = { has_id = 2504 } } }

	}
}

country_event = { #buff ally
	id = zizhi_hidden_event.7
	hidden = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 30 }
	title = ""
	desc = ""
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		TAG = ENG
		has_War_with = GER
		OR = { date > 1943.1.1 should_ally_do_dday = yes }
		has_war_with_human_player = no
		is_historical_focus_on = yes
	}
	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = yes
				is_in_faction_with = ENG
				OR = { TAG = ENG TAG = USA TAG = CAN TAG = AST TAG = FRA TAG = POL }
			}
			add_ideas = balance_idea_buff_ally
			add_to_variable = {
		    var = This.supply_condition
			value = 500 #MODDED
		    }
		    add_to_variable = {
			var = This.supply_condition_base
			value = 500 #MODDED
		    }
			add_to_variable = {
				Root.supply_condition_base = 500
			}
		}
	}
}
